of_IN the_DT milk_NN used_VBN in_IN cities_NNS of_IN 10,000_CD population_NN and_CC over_PRP is_VBZ pasteurized_VBN ._.

The_DT question_NN of_IN whether_IN pasteurized_JJ milk_NN is_VBZ equal_JJ nutritionally_RB to_TO raw_VB milk_NN is_VBZ far_RB from_IN settled_VBN at_IN the_DT present_JJ time_NN ,_, and_CC each_DT new_JJ investigation_NN seems_VBZ to_TO increase_VB the_DT discordance_NN in_IN results_NNS ._.

[_NN V_NNP ,_, II_NNP that_IN rats_NNS reared_VBD from_IN weaning_VBG on_IN whole_JJ cow_NN 's_POS milk_NN mineralized_VBN with_IN iron_NN ,_, copper_NN ,_, and_CC manganese_JJ grew_VBD from_IN 60-200_JJ gm_NN ._.

EXPERIMENTAL_NNP ._.
The_DT milk_NN used_VBN throughout_IN these_DT experiments_NNS was_VBD received_VBN directly_RB from_IN the_DT University_NNP of_IN Wisconsin_NNP Dairy_NNP each_DT day_NN ._.

in_IN a_DT vat_NN and_CC held_VBD at_IN that_DT temperature_NN for_IN 30_CD minutes_NNS ._.
*_NN It_PRP was_VBD then_RB cooled_VBN over_RP a_DT surface_NN cooler_NN to_TO 40°_CD F._NNP The_DT two_CD milks_NNS were_VBD therefore_RB identical_JJ except_IN for_IN the_DT pasteurization_NN process_NN ._.
The_DT first_JJ feeding_NN trial_NN ,_, which_WDT will_MD be_VB described_VBN in_IN detail_NN ,_, was_VBD started_VBN October_NNP 26_CD ,_, 1932_CD ._.
Three_CD litters_NNS of_IN six_CD rats_NNS each_DT were_VBD taken_VBN from_IN the_DT stock_NN colony_NN at_IN weaning_NN ._.

INTRODUCTION_NN Of_IN the_DT chronic_JJ diseases_NNS of_IN the_DT bovine_NN skin_NN in_IN India_NNP ,_, hump_NN sore_NN is_VBZ one_CD that_WDT has_VBZ for_IN many_JJ years_NNS baffled_VBD the_DT attempts_NNS of_IN field_NN veterinary_JJ workers_NNS to_TO elucidate_VB its_PRP$ cause_NN and_CC provide_VB an_DT efficient_JJ method_NN of_IN treatment_NN ._.

Three_CD types_NNS of_IN lesions_NNS have_VBP been_VBN recognised_VBN depending_VBG upon_IN the_DT time_NN of_IN the_DT year_NN and_CC the_DT stage_NN of_IN development_NN ._.

INTRODUCTION_NNP ._.
